beginSubroutine: s32'CmnCutSceneDamage_Kakusei'
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'pot'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'pot', 0, 0
  endIf: 
  ifOpponentCharacterMain: s16'fau'
  if: Mem(Tmp)
    debugLogForScript: s32'fau', 0, 0
  endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'WFree_KobetsuFunc'
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'OnFrameStep'
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnOnFrameStep'
  if: Val(3)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(5000)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge2), Val(50)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(5000)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge2), Val(50)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(10000)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge2), Val(50)
    endIf: 
    modifyVar2: (DIV), Val(15000), Val(3)
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      if: Mem(ExGauge1)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(0)
      endIf: 
    endElse: 
    ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
      ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
        ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
          if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(PlayerVal3), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          if: Mem(ExGauge3)
            modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge3), Val(1)
            if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
              modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge3), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
              if: Val(300)
                modifyVar2: (DIV), Val(15000), Val(300)
                modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(Tmp), Mem(ExGauge2)
                modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(Tmp)
                if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
                  modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(Tmp), Val(2)
                  modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(Tmp)
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
              else: 
                modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
              storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(0)
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(AdjustmentForScript3), Val(-1)
    storeValue: Mem(ExGauge1), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(ObjReg1)
    ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
      ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
        ifNot: Mem(CheckStop)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(-1)
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
            walkFSpeed: 6800
            walkBSpeed: 5150
            initDashFSpeed: 14500
            fDashAccelSpeed: 580
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(2)
            walkFSpeed: 7300
            walkBSpeed: 5400
            initDashFSpeed: 15000
            fDashAccelSpeed: 600
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(3)
            walkFSpeed: 7800
            walkBSpeed: 5650
            initDashFSpeed: 15500
            fDashAccelSpeed: 620
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(4)
            walkFSpeed: 8300
            walkBSpeed: 5900
            initDashFSpeed: 16000
            fDashAccelSpeed: 640
          endIf: 
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(5)
            walkFSpeed: 8800
            walkBSpeed: 6150
            initDashFSpeed: 16500
            fDashAccelSpeed: 660
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
    walkFSpeed: 6300
    walkBSpeed: 4900
    initDashFSpeed: 14000
    fDashAccelSpeed: 560
  endElse: 
  if: Mem(PlayerVal3)
    isObjectActive: (STACK0)
    ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
      exPointFReset: (PLAYER), 0, 150000
      createObject: s32'SIN_408_buff_Aura', (EX_POINT_F)
      stackObject: (STACK0), (PREVIOUS)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_SIN', 2, 157
  ifOperation: (AND), Mem(TrainingValue), Mem(IsMainPlayerSelf)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(1)
      if: Mem(IsRecoverableTypeA)
        storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(TrainingValue), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(15000)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

    storeValue: Mem(ExGauge3), Val(240)
  endIf:

beginSubroutine: s32'StillGrowing'
  setRandom: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1), Val(15)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(15)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(AdjustmentForScript1)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Mem(AdjustmentForScript1)
  endIf: 
  setRandom: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1), Val(15)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(15)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(6)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(3)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(4)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(5)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(AdjustmentForScript2)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Mem(AdjustmentForScript2)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(60)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(60)
    sendValuesToObject: 2, 47, 2, 48
    createObjectWithArg: s32'StillGrowing_buffA', (PLAYER)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
    storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Mem(ActReg2)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(60), Mem(ObjReg1)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg1), Val(60)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(300)
    addTensionUnscaled: 2, 47
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(4)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(60)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(60)
    sendValuesToObject: 2, 47, 2, 48
    createObjectWithArg: s32'StillGrowing_buffB', (PLAYER)
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(5)
    modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(HitPoint), Mem(ActReg2)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'RTL_Move_Accel'
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
  upon: (IDLING)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(3)
      velocityXPercentEachFrame: 85
      velocityYPercentEachFrame: 85
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(12)
      velocityXPercentEachFrame: 80
      velocityYPercentEachFrame: 80
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(18)
      velocityXPercentEachFrame: 100
      velocityYPercentEachFrame: 100
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ActReg5)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PosY), Val(300000)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(OnIdlingTime), Val(0)
          velocityXPercent: 50
          velocityYPercent: 50
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(IsAir)
        velocityXPercentEachFrame: 90
        velocityYPercentEachFrame: 90
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'RTL_Rush_Input'
  if: Mem(CPUVal0)
    storeValue: Mem(CPUVal1), Val(0)
  endIf: 
  upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
    checkInput: 29
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      endIf: 
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Mem(Dir)
      checkInput: (INPUT_1)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_2)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_3)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_4)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_5)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_6)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_7)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(7)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_8)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(8)
      endIf: 
      checkInput: (INPUT_9)
      if: Mem(Tmp)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(9)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(IsCPU)
      if: Mem(CPUVal0)
        ifNot: Mem(CPUVal1)
          setRandom: Mem(CPUVal1), Val(1), Val(12)
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(CPUVal1), Val(1)
            ifNot: Mem(Dir)
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)
            endIf: 
            else: 
              storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
            endElse: 
          endIf:

            endElse:

            endElse: 
          endIf:

              ifNot: Mem(Dir)
                storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
              endIf:

                storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
              endElse:

                storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)

beginSubroutine: s32'RTL_Rush_Start'
  enableGatlings: 0
  upon: (FRAME_STEP)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_maincheck', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    if: Mem(ReturnValue)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ActReg0)
      if: Mem(ActReg2)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (FRAME_STEP)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
          enableGatlings: 1
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
          ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Mem(Dir)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
              if: Mem(IsAir)
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'1'
              endIf: 
              else: 
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'4'
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
              if: Mem(IsAir)
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'2'
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
              if: Mem(IsAir)
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'3'
              endIf: 
              else: 
                gotoLabelRequests: s32'6'
              endElse: 
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'4'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'6'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(7)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'7'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(8)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'8'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(9)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'9'
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'3'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'2'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'1'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'6'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'4'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(7)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'9'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(8)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'8'
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(9)
              gotoLabelRequests: s32'7'
            endIf: 
          endElse: 
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'RTL_Rush_End'
  recoveryState: 
  if: Mem(IsAir)
    upon: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (TOUCH_GROUND)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end_land'
    endUpon: 
    resetGravity: 
    setGravity: 3000
    ifNot: Mem(ActReg5)
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end_air'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      gotoLabelRequests: s32'end_air123'
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    gotoLabelRequests: s32'end_land'
  endElse: 
endSubroutine:

beginSubroutine: s32'RTLA_setting'
  modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(Tension), Val(100), Mem(ActReg1)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(24)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(49)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
  ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(50)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)

  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(100)
